            function CNNIC_RndNum(k) {
                var rnd = "";
                for (var i = 0; i < k; i++) rnd += Math.floor(Math.random() * 10);
                return rnd;

<script>var weekRank2Effect = function (){
    var firstNode = $("#weekRank li").eq(0);

    function  bindEvent(linode,i){
        linode.bind('mouseover',function(){
            if( i != 0 ) {
                firstNode.removeClass('fore').find('.p-img').hide();
                firstNode.find('.p-price').hide();

                linode.addClass('fore').find('.p-img').show();
                linode.find('.p-price').show();
            }
        }).bind('mouseout',function(){
                if( i != 0 ) {
                    linode.removeClass('fore').find('.p-img').hide();
                    linode.find('.p-price').hide();

                    firstNode.addClass('fore').find('.p-img').show();
                    firstNode.find('.p-price').show();
                }
            });
    }
    $("#weekRank").find("li").each(function(i){
        var linode = $(this);
        bindEvent(linode,i);
    });
};

weekRank2Effect();

function refreshPrice(area) {
    var skuids = [],
        hotSalePriceQ = $("#hotsale .p-price"),
        weekRankPriceQ = $("#weekRank .p-price"),
        skuId;

    for (var i = 0, l=hotSalePriceQ.length; i < l; i++) {
        skuId = hotSalePriceQ.eq(i).attr('sku');
        if ( skuId ) {
            skuids.push( skuId );
        }
    }
    for (var i = 0, l=weekRankPriceQ.length; i < l; i++) {
        skuId = weekRankPriceQ.eq(i).attr('sku');
        if ( skuId ) {
            skuids.push( skuId );
        }
    }

    function getPrice(skuids) {
        if ( !skuids || skuids.length == 0 ) {
            return;
        }


        $.ajax({
            url: 'http://p.3.cn/prices/mgets?skuIds=J_' + skuids.join(',J_') + '&type=1&area='+area,
            dataType: 'jsonp',
            success: function(r) {
                if ( !r && !r.length ) { return false; }
                for ( var i = 0; i < r.length; i++ ) {
                    var sku = r[i].id.replace('J_', '');
                    var price = r[i].p;
                    if ( price > 0 ) {
                        $(".p-price[sku='"+sku+"']").children("strong").html( '\uffe5' + price);
                    } else {
                        $(".p-price[sku='"+sku+"']").children("strong").html( '暂无报价' );
                    }
                }
            }
        });
    }
    getPrice(skuids);
};
var areaStr = params.area.split(',').join('-');
refreshPrice(areaStr);</script><script>$("#pipe_1769578722305596_1403765974760").replaceWith("<div id=\"limitbuy1326\" clstag=\"thirdtype|keycount|thirdtype|limitbuy536\" class=\"m limitbuy hide\"><div class=\"mt\"><h2>家居生活</h2></div><div class=\"mc\"><div id=\"clock1326\" class=\"clock\">正在加载…</div><div id=\"limit1326\"></div></div></div>")</script>

<script>if( window.screen.width < 1210 ) {
    $('div[rel]').each(function(i){
        if( i>=12 ) {
            $(this).attr('more','true');
            $(this).hide();
        } else {
            $(this).attr('more','false');
        }
    });

}

$('.brand-attr li[rel]:not(:first)').each(function(){
    var rel = $(this).attr('rel');
    if ( $('.brand-attr .tabcon div[rel=' + rel + ']').length == 0 ) {
        $(this).hide();
    }

});

$('li[rel]').bind('mouseover',function(){
    var rel = $(this).attr('rel');
    $(this).addClass('curr');
    $('li:not([rel='+rel+'])').removeClass('curr');

    if( rel==0 ) {
        $('div[rel]').show();
    } else {
        $('div[rel='+rel+']').show();
        $('div[rel]:not([rel='+rel+'])').hide();

    }
});

$('.prop-attrs:not(.hide) .f-list').each(function(){

    if( $(this).find('li:last').position().top > 0 ){
        $(this).parent().parent().find('[option=more]').show();
    }

});

$(".show-logo div:not(.curr)").bind("mouseover",function(){
    $(this).addClass("hover");
}).bind("mouseout",function(){
        $(this).removeClass("hover")
    });

function moreProp(t){
    $(t).hide();
    $('#lessProp').show();

    $('[overfour=true]').show();

    $('.prop-attrs[overfour=true] .f-list').each(function(){

        if( $(this).find('li:last').position().top > 0 ){
            $(this).parent().parent().find('[option=more]').show();
        }

    });
}

function lessProp(t){
    $(t).hide();
    $('#moreProp').show();
    $('[overfour=true]').hide();

}

function moreBrand(){
    $('.brand-attr ul.tab').show();

    $('.brand-attr [option=more]').hide();
    $('.brand-attr [option=less]').show();

    $('.brand-attr div[more=true]').show();

    $('.brand-attr div.tabcon').addClass('tabcon-multi');
    if(psid3 == 655) {
        $('.brand-attr div.tabcon').addClass('height185');
    }


    $('li[rel].curr').removeClass('curr');
    $('li[rel]:first').addClass('curr');
}



function lessBrand(){
    $('.brand-attr ul.tab').hide();

    $('.brand-attr [option=more]').show();
    $('.brand-attr [option=less]').hide();

    $('.brand-attr div[more=false]').show();
    $('.brand-attr div[more=true]').hide();

    $('.brand-attr div.tabcon').removeClass('tabcon-multi');
    if(psid3 == 655) {
        $('.brand-attr div.tabcon').removeClass('height185');
    }

}
function moreExpandValue(t){
    $(t).hide().next().show();
    $(t).parent().find('.v-fold').addClass('v-unfold');

}
function lessExpandValue(t){
    $(t).parent().find('.v-fold').removeClass('v-unfold');
    $(t).hide().prev().show();

}

// 日历
var  currYear  = new Date().getFullYear();
var cal = $('input.txt-birthday').Jcal({
    chosendate: (new Date().getMonth()+1) + '/' + (new Date().getDate()) + '/' + new Date().getFullYear(),
    startdate: '1/1/'+(currYear-14),
    enddate: '12/31/'+(currYear+1),
    outputFormat: '{y}-{m}-{d}',
    x: -142,
    y: 0
});

$('#babyQueryAttr a.boy').click(function(){
    $(this).toggleClass('selected')
    $('#babyQueryAttr a.girl').toggleClass('selected')
})

$('#babyQueryAttr a.girl').click(function(){
    $(this).toggleClass('selected')
    $('#babyQueryAttr a.boy').toggleClass('selected')

})


function get_baby_info(){
    var el_baby = $('#babyQueryAttr'), bb_birthday,bb_gender=0,bb_height='',bb_weight='',birthday_input=el_baby.find(".txt-birthday"), now = new Date();
    if( !el_baby.length ) { return; }
    if( !birthday_input.attr('data-init') ) {
        birthday_input.Jcal({
            chosendate: (now.getMonth()+1)+'/'+now.getDate()+'/'+now.getFullYear(),
            startdate: (now.getMonth()+1)+'/'+now.getDate()+'/'+(now.getFullYear()-14),
            enddate: (now.getMonth()+1)+'/'+now.getDate()+'/'+(now.getFullYear()+1),
            outputFormat: '{y}-{m}-{d}',
            zIndex: 10, x:0, y:0
        });
        birthday_input.attr('data-init','1'); //防止重复绑定
    }
    function gen_tip(birthday) {
        var birthday = new Date(birthday*1), res={'tip':''}, t1,t2;
        t1 = birthday<now ? birthday : now;
        t2 = birthday<now ? now : birthday;
        var y=t2.getYear()-t1.getYear(), m=t2.getMonth()-t1.getMonth(), d=t2.getDate()-t1.getDate();
        if( d<0 ) { d+=30; m-=1; }
        if( m<0 ) { m+=12; y-=1; }
        if( !y && !m && !d ) {
            res = { 'tip':'即将出生', 'status':'now'};
        } else if (birthday<now) {
            res['status'] = 'past';
            if( y ) {
                res.tip = y+'岁' + (m ? m+'个月': '' );
            } else {
                if( m ) { res.tip = m+'个月'; }
                if( d ) { res.tip += d+'天'; }
            }
        } else {
            res['status'] = 'future';
            if( y ) {
                res.tip = y+'年' + (m ? m+'个月': '' );
            } else {
                if( m ) { res.tip = m+'个月'; }
                if( d ) { res.tip += d+'天'; }
            }
        }
        if( res['status']=='now' ) {
            el_baby.find('.tc-info').html('您的宝宝<strong>即将出生</strong>啦！<a href="javascript:;" class="tci-change" clstag="search|keycount|search|updatebabyinfo">[ 修改信息 ]</a>');
        } else if( res.status=='past' ) {
            el_baby.find('.tc-info').html('您的宝宝已经<strong>'+res.tip+'</strong>啦！<a href="javascript:;" class="tci-change" clstag="search|keycount|search|updatebabyinfo">[ 修改信息 ]</a>');
        } else if( res.status=='future' ) {
            el_baby.find('.tc-info').html('您的宝宝即将在<strong>'+res.tip+'</strong>后出生！<a href="javascript:;" class="tci-change" clstag="search|keycount|search|updatebabyinfo">[ 修改信息 ]</a>');
        }
        el_baby.find('.tc-info a').click(function(){
            el_baby.find('.query-con').removeClass('hide');
            el_baby.find('.tips-con').addClass('hide');
        });
        $('#babyQueryAttr').removeClass('hide');
    }


    function filtUrl(d, c) {
        var e, f;
        if (!d && !c) {
            return ""
        } else {
            if (!c) {
                e = window.location.pathname + window.location.search;
                f = d
            } else {
                e = d;
                f = c
            }
        }
        return e.replace(new RegExp("(^|\\?|&)" + f + "=([^&]*)", "gi"), "")
    }

    function set_bb_info(bb_birthday, bb_gender) {
        var param = bb_birthday+'-'+bb_height+'-'+bb_weight+'-'+bb_gender;
        $.ajax({
            url:'http://uprofile.jd.com/u/baby/setinfo?babyinfo='+param,
            async:true,
            dataType: 'jsonp',
            success:function(data){
                if(!data||data.flag!=2){alert('Joy,没记住您的选择...'); return;}
                gen_tip(bb_birthday);
                el_baby.find('.query-con').addClass('hide');
                el_baby.find('.tips-con').removeClass('hide');
                if( $('#for_my_bb').hasClass('tc-btn-selected') ) {
                    var url = filtUrl(window.location.href,'baby');
                    window.location.href= url;
                }
            }
        });
    }
    //1：代表男，2：代表女
    $.ajax({
        url:'http://uprofile.jd.com/u/baby/getinfo?callback=?',
        async:true,
        dataType:'jsonp',
        success:function(data){
            var data = data.babyinfo.split('-');
            if( !data || !data[0] ) { el_baby.removeClass('hide').find('.query-con').removeClass('hide'); return ; }
            bb_birthday=data[0];
            bb_height=data[1];
            bb_weight=data[2];
            bb_gender=data[3]||0;
            el_baby.find('.tips-con').removeClass('hide');
            var bd = new Date(bb_birthday*1);
            el_baby.find('.query-con .txt-birthday').val(bd.getFullYear()+'-'+(bd.getMonth()+1)+'-'+bd.getDate());
            if(bb_gender=='1') { el_baby.find('.query-con .boy').addClass('selected'); }
            if(bb_gender=='2') { el_baby.find('.query-con .girl').addClass('selected'); }
            gen_tip(data[0]);
        }
    });
    $('#for_my_bb').click(function(){
        var url = window.location.href
        if( !$(this).hasClass('tc-btn-selected') ) {
            url += '&baby='+bb_birthday+','+bb_gender;
        } else {
            url = filtUrl(window.location.href,'baby');
        }
        window.location.href = url;
    });
    el_baby.find('.boy').click(function(){
        $(this).addClass('selected');
        el_baby.find('.girl').removeClass('selected');
    });
    el_baby.find('.girl').click(function(){
        $(this).addClass('selected');
        el_baby.find('.boy').removeClass('selected');
    });
    el_baby.find('.btn-submit').click(function(){
        var birthday = $.trim(el_baby.find('.txt-birthday').val());
        if( !birthday ) { alert('请选择宝宝出生日期'); return; }
        if( !/^(\d{4})-(\d{1,2})-(\d{1,2})$/.test(birthday) ) {
            alert('Joy看不懂您写的日期，请按照"年-月-日"格式书写');
            return;
        }
        bb_birthday = new Date(RegExp.$1,RegExp.$2-1,RegExp.$3).getTime();
        if( el_baby.find('.boy').hasClass('selected') ) { bb_gender=1; }
        if( el_baby.find('.girl').hasClass('selected') ) { bb_gender=2; }
        jdModelCallCenter.settings.fn=function(){
            set_bb_info(bb_birthday, bb_gender);
        }
        $.getJSON("http://passport.jd.com/loginservice.aspx?method=Login&callback=?", function(r) {
            if (r && r.Identity && r.Identity.IsAuthenticated) {
                set_bb_info(bb_birthday, bb_gender);
            } else {
                jdModelCallCenter.login();
            }
        });
        $('.Jcalendar').remove();
    });
}

get_baby_info();
/* 母婴 end */

var selectedProvinceId,selectedCityId,selectedAreaId,selectedProvinceId,selectedCityName,selectedAreaName;


function getAreaStoreUrl(areaId){
    var reg = new RegExp("(^|&)area=([^&]+)(&|$)", "g");
    var match =  window.location.search.substr(1).match(reg)

    var areaParam = '&area=' + selectedProvinceId + ',' + selectedCityId + ',' + areaId;

    if( match && match.length > 0 ) {
        match = match[0];
        if(match.substr(match.length - 1,1) == '&') {
            match = match.substr(0,match.length -1)
        }

        return window.location.href.replace( match, areaParam );
    } else {
        return 'http://'+ window.location.hostname +':' + window.location.port+'/list.html' + window.location.search + areaParam;
    }


}

function selectStoreTab(index) {
    if(index == 0) {
        $('dl.store div.mt li').eq(0).find('em').text('请选择');
        $('dl.store div.mt li').eq(1).addClass('hide').find('em').text("请选择");
        $('dl.store div.mt li').eq(2).addClass('hide').find('em').text("请选择");;
        $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(0).addClass('curr');
        $('dl.store [data-area="0"]').removeClass('hide');
        $('dl.store [data-area="1"]').addClass('hide');
        $('dl.store [data-area="2"]').addClass('hide');

    } else if(index == 1) {
        $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(1).addClass('curr').find('em').text('请选择');

        $('dl.store [data-area="1"]').removeClass('hide');

        $('dl.store div.mt li').eq(2).addClass('hide').find('em').text('请选择');
        $('dl.store [data-area="2"]').addClass('hide');

    } else if(index == 2) {
    }
}

function getAreaList_callback(data){
    $('dl.store div[data-area="1"]').addClass('hide');
    $('dl.store div[data-area="2"]').removeClass('hide');
    $('dl.store div[data-area="2"] p.ac').addClass('hide');


    var thirdTabPanel = $('dl.store div.mc[data-area="2"] ul').empty();
    var areaStr="",
        areaLongStr="",
        areaLongerStr="";

    for(var i = 0;i < data.length; i++){
        var item = data[i];
        var name = item['name'];
        var url = getAreaStoreUrl(item['id']);
        if(name.length <= 5){
            areaStr += "<li><a data-value='" + item['id'] + "' href='" + url + "'>" + item['name'] + "</a></li>";
        }else if(name.length <= 11){
            areaLongStr += "<li class='long-area'><a data-value='" + item['id'] + "' href='" + url + "'>" + item['name'] + "</a></li>";
        } else  {
            areaLongerStr += "<li class='longer-area'><a data-value='" + item['id'] + "' href='" + url + "'>" + item['name'] + "</a></li>";
        }
    }

    thirdTabPanel.append(areaStr + areaLongStr + areaLongerStr);
}


function selectProvince(parentId,name){

    selectedProvinceId = parentId;
    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(0).removeClass('curr');
    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(0).find('em').text(name);
    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(1).removeClass('hide').addClass('curr');
    $('dl.store [data-area="0"]').addClass('hide');
    $('dl.store [data-area="1"]').removeClass('hide');
    $('dl.store [data-area="1"] p.ac').addClass('hide');


    var secondTabPanel = $('dl.store div.mc[data-area="1"] ul').empty();
    var thirdTabPanel = $('dl.store div.mc[data-area="2"] ul').empty();
    $('dl.store [data-area="2"] p.ac').removeClass('hide');


    var selectCityArray = provinceCityJson[parentId];
    var areaStr="",
        areaLongStr="",
        areaLongerStr="";
    for (var i=0; i < selectCityArray.length; i++) {
        var name = selectCityArray[i]['name'];
        var id = selectCityArray[i]['id'];

        if(name.length <= 5){
            areaStr += "<li><a data-value='" + id + "' href='#none' onclick='selectCity(" + id + ",\"" + name + "\")'>" + name + "</a></li>";
        } else if( name.length <= 11 ) {
            areaLongStr += "<li class='long-area'><a data-value='" + id + "' onclick='selectCity(" + id +  ",\"" + name + "\")' href='#none'>" + name + "</a></li>";
        }else {
            areaLongerStr += "<li class='longer-area'><a data-value='" + id + "' onclick='selectCity(" + id +  ",\"" + name + "\")' href='#none'>" + name + "</a></li>";
        }
    }

    secondTabPanel.append(areaStr + areaLongStr + areaLongerStr);
}

function selectCity(parentId,name) {
    selectedCityId = parentId;

    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(1).removeClass('curr');
    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(1).find('em').text(name);
    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(2).removeClass('hide').addClass('curr');




    $.ajax({
        url:'http://d.360buy.com/area/get?fid=' + parentId + '&callback=getAreaList_callback',
        dataType:'jsonp'
    });
}


function getAreaName_callback(data){
    for(var i = 0;i < data.length; i++){
        var item = data[i];
        if(item['id'] == selectedAreaId) {
            selectedAreaName = item['name'];
            break;
        }

    }

    if(!selectedAreaName) {
        selectedAreaId = data[0]['id'];
        selectedAreaName = data[0]['name'];
    }

    $('dl.store [data-widget=tab-item]').eq(2).find('em').text(selectedAreaName);

    if(selectedProvinceName && selectedCityName && selectedAreaName){
        $('#store-selector div.text').html(selectedProvinceName + selectedCityName + selectedAreaName + "<b></b>");
    }
}



$('#store-selector div.text').bind('mouseover',function(){
    $('#store-selector').addClass('hover');
});

$('body').click(function(g) {
    var d = g.srcElement || g.target,
        connectDom = [$('#store-selector').get(0)];
    while (d) {
        for (var f = 0; f < connectDom.length; f++) {
            if (d == connectDom[f]) {
                return
            }
        }
        if (d === document.body) {
            $('#store-selector').removeClass('hover');
            return
        }
        d = d.parentNode;
    }
})


var area = params.area.split(',');
selectedProvinceId = area[0];
selectedCityId = area[1];
selectedAreaId = area[2];

selectedProvinceName = iplocation[selectedProvinceId]['name'];

if( !selectedProvinceName ){
    selectedProvinceName = iplocation[1]['name'];
    selectedProvinceId = 1;
}


var citysInProvince = provinceCityJson[selectedProvinceId];
for(var i = 0; i < citysInProvince.length; i++) {
    if(selectedCityId == citysInProvince[i]['id']) {
        selectedCityName =  citysInProvince[i]['name'];
        break;
    }
}
if( !selectedCityName ){
    selectedCityName = citysInProvince[0]['name'];
    selectedCityId = citysInProvince[0]['id'];
}


selectProvince(selectedProvinceId,selectedProvinceName);
selectCity(selectedCityId,selectedCityName);

$.getJSONP('http://d.360buy.com/area/get?fid=' + selectedCityId + '&callback=getAreaName_callback');



var firstTabPanel = $('dl.store div.mc[data-area="0"] ul');
for(var id in iplocation) {
    var name = iplocation[id]['name'];
    if(name.length <= 4){
        firstTabPanel.append("<li><a data-value='" + id + "' href='#none' onclick='selectProvince(" + id + ",\"" + name + "\")'>" + name + "</a></li>");
    } else {
        firstTabPanel.append("<li class='long-area'><a data-value='" + id + "' onclick='selectProvince(" + id + ",\"" + name + "\")' href='#none'>" + name + "</a></li>");
    }
}

<script>//收集skuId
var skuIds = [];
$('ul.list-h li[sku]').each(function(i){
    skuIds.push($(this).attr('sku'));
})


/* 实时价格 begin*/
function getPrice(skuIds) {
    if ( !skuIds || skuIds.length == 0 ) {
        return;
    }


    $.ajax({
        url: 'http://p.3.cn/prices/mgets?skuIds=J_' + skuIds.join(',J_') + '&type=1&area='+params.area,
        dataType: 'jsonp',
        success: function(r) {
            if ( !r && !r.length ) { return false; }
            for ( var i = 0; i < r.length; i++ ) {
                var sku = r[i].id.replace('J_', '');
                var price = r[i].p;
                if ( price > 0 ) {
                    $("li[sku='"+sku+"'] .p-price").children("strong").html( '\uffe5' + price);
                } else {
                    $("li[sku='"+sku+"'] .p-price").children("strong").html( '暂无报价' );
                }
            }
        }
    });
}


getPrice(skuIds);
/* 实时价格 end */


/* 促销标签 begin*/
function getPromotionTag(json) {
    if (!json){return;}
    var pInfo,prdbuy;
    for (var i=0;i<json.length;i++){
        pInfo="";
        prdbuy = $("#p"+json[i].pid+" .pt5").length>0;
        for (var j=0;j<json[i].pf.length;j++){
            pInfo=null;
            switch (json[i].pf[j]){
                case 22:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt1\" title=\"使用京豆可享受优惠\">优惠购</a>";
                    break;
                case 11:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt1\" title=\"指定级别会员可享受优惠\">特价</a>";
                    break;
                case 1:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt1\" title=\"本商品正在降价销售中\">直降</a>";
                    break;
                case 5:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt2\" title=\"购买本商品送赠品\">赠品</a>";
                    break;
                case 3:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt3\" title=\"购买本商品返优惠券\">返券</a>";
                    break;
                case 4:
                    pInfo = "<a class=\"pt4\" title=\"购买本商品送京豆\">送京豆</a>";
                    break;
                default:
                    break;
            }
            //if(prdbuy&&pInfo){$(pInfo).insertBefore("#p"+json[i].pid+" .pt5");break;}
            if(pInfo){
                $(pInfo).prependTo("span#p"+json[i].pid);
            }

        }
        //if(!prdbuy)$("#p"+json[i].pid).html(pInfo);
    }
}

(function(){
    var skuIdsForFlags = skuIds.join(',J_') ;
    $.getJSONP('http://ad.3.cn/flags/mgets?skuids=J_' + skuIdsForFlags);

})();

/* 促销标签 end*/

/* 广告词 begin*/

function strip_tags (input, allowed) {
    allowed = (((allowed || "") + "").toLowerCase().match(/<[a-z][a-z0-9]*>/g) || []).join(''); // making sure the allowed arg is a string containing only tags in lowercase (<a><b><c>)
    var tags = /<\/?([a-z][a-z0-9]*)\b[^>]*>/gi,
        commentsAndPhpTags = /<!--[\s\S]*?-->|<\?(?:php)?[\s\S]*?\?>/gi;
    return input.replace(commentsAndPhpTags, '').replace(tags, function ($0, $1) {
        return allowed.indexOf('<' + $1.toLowerCase() + '>') > -1 ? $0 : '';
    });
}

var GetJdwsmentsCallback = function(json) {
    for (var i=0; i<json.length; i++) {
        var wid  = json[i].id.split("_")[1];
        var object=$("#plist li[sku='"+ wid  +"']"),adTitle=json[i].ad;
        if (object.length){
            if ( !!adTitle.replace(/\s+/g, '') ) {
                object.find(".p-img").find("img").attr("title",strip_tags(adTitle));
                object.find(".p-name").find("a").attr("title",strip_tags(adTitle));
                object.find(".adwords").html(strip_tags(adTitle));
            }
        }
    }
};

(function(){
    var skuIdsForAds = skuIds.join(',AD_')
    $.getJSONP('http://ad.3.cn/ads/mgets?skuids=AD_'+ skuIdsForAds +'&callback=GetJdwsmentsCallback');

})();
/* 广告词 begin*/


/* 库存信息 begin*/


function get_stock_cb(json) {
    if( !json || typeof json!='object' ) { return; }
    var el_infos = $('div.stocklist[stock]'),stock= selectedProvinceId + '-' + selectedCityId + '-' + selectedAreaId, city= iplocation[selectedProvinceId]['name'] ||'';
    for( var i=0,l=el_infos.length; i<l; i++ ) {
        var el_info=el_infos.eq(i);
        var wid =el_info.attr('stock'), info = json[wid], class_name='btn btn-nostore notice-store', el_btn = el_info.parent().find('a.btn-buy');

        if( !info ) { continue; }


        switch( info['stockvalue'] & 0xffff ) {
            case 0  :
            case 18 :
            case 33 :
                el_info && el_info.html('<span class="st33">'+city+'有货</span>');
                break;
            case 34 :
                el_btn.attr({'href':'javascript:;','class':class_name,'data-type':2,'data-sku':wid,'id':'store'+wid}).removeAttr('target').html('<b></b>到货通知');
                el_info && el_info.html('<span class="st34">'+city+'无货</span>');
                break;
            case 36 :
                el_info && el_info.html('<span class="st36">'+city+'预定</span>');
                break;
            case 40 :
                el_info && el_info.html('<span class="st40">'+city+'有货 <b>下单后2-6天发货</b></span>');
                break;
            default : break;
        }
    }

    NotifyPop.init( $(".notice-store") );
}

function get_stock() {
    var el = $('a[stock]'),area = params.area;
    $.getJSONP('http://search.jd.com/stock?skus=' + encodeURIComponent(skuIds.join(',')) + '&district=' + area.replace(',','_').replace(',','_') +  '&callback=get_stock_cb');
}

get_stock()
/* 库存信息 end*/


/*预售 begin*/
var yushouSkuIds = [];
$('ul.list-h li[selfservice=2]').each(function(i){
    yushouSkuIds.push($(this).attr('sku'));
})

var yushouTimerList = [];
function convertSecond2Date(ms) {//将毫秒数换算成x天x时x分x秒x毫秒
    var mi = 60;
    var hh = mi * 60;
    var dd = hh * 24;

    var day = Math.floor(ms / dd);
    var hour = Math.floor((ms - day * dd) / hh);
    var minute = Math.floor((ms - day * dd - hour * hh) / mi);
    var second = Math.floor(ms - day * dd - hour * hh - minute * mi);

    if(day == 0) {
        return hour + "时" + minute + "分" + second + "秒";
    }else{
        return day + "天" + hour + "时" + minute + "分";
    }
}

if(yushouSkuIds) {

    for( var i = 0; i < yushouSkuIds.length; i++ ) {
        var skuId = yushouSkuIds[i];

        if(skuId&&skuId!=""){
            $.getJSONP('http://soa.yushou.jd.com/yushoulistinfo.action?sku=' + skuId + '&callback=yushouCallback');
        }
    }
}


function showYushouTime(){
    for(var i = 0; i < yushouTimerList.length; i++){
        var yushowTimer = yushouTimerList[i];
        yushowTimer.d--;
        if(yushowTimer.t < 0){
            return;
        }

        var yushouEl = $('#plist .list-h li[sku=' + yushowTimer.w + ']');
        if( yushowTimer.s == 0 ) {
            yushouEl.find('.p-img a em').html(convertSecond2Date(yushowTimer.d)+"后开始");

        } else {
            yushouEl.find('.p-img a em').html('剩余'+convertSecond2Date(yushowTimer.d));
        }


    }
    setTimeout(showYushouTime,1000);

}

setTimeout(showYushouTime,1000);

function yushouCallback( data ){

    if(data.type == 2){
        var ret = data.ret;
        var skuId = ret.w;
        var yushouEl = $('#plist .list-h li[sku=' + skuId + ']');

        yushouTimerList[yushouTimerList.length] = {w:skuId,d:ret.d,s:ret.s};
        if( ret.s == 0 ) {
            yushouEl.find('.p-img a').append('<div class="prebuy-time"><div class="pt-bg"></div><i></i><span>等待预售</span><em>' + convertSecond2Date(data.ret.d) + '后开始</em></div>');

        } else {
            yushouEl.find('.p-img a').append('<div class="prebuy-time"><div class="pt-bg"></div><i></i><span>预售中</span><em>剩余' + convertSecond2Date(data.ret.d) + '</em></div>');

        }


        if (ret.t==2 ){
            var html = '<div clstag="" class="sp-stage clearfix">';

            for(var i = 0; i < ret.sa.length; i++) {
                var sa = ret.sa[i];
                var currCls = "";
                var timeoutCls = "";

                var hoverd = "";
                if ( i == (ret.cs-1) ) {
                    currCls = " curr";
                    hoverd = '<em class="hoverd">预订' + ret.cc + '人</em>';
                }

                html += '<span class="item  ' + currCls + '"><a href="javascript:void(0)"><em>满' + sa.c + '人</em>' + hoverd + '<strong>￥' + sa.m + '</strong></a><i class="bottom"><em></em></i></span>';
            }

            html += '</div>'

            $(html).insertAfter(yushouEl.find('.p-price'));

        }


        yushouEl.find('.p-price').append('<i class="prebuy-num">（已有' + ret.cc + '人预订）</i>');
        yushouEl.find('.p-price strong').html(ret.cp);

        yushouEl.find('.btn-buy').attr('href','http://cart.jd.com/cart/dynamic/presale.action?pid=' + skuId + '&pcount=1&ptype=1');


        if( ret.s == 0 ) {
            yushouEl.find('.btn-buy').text('等待支付定金').addClass('disable');
        } else {
            yushouEl.find('.btn-buy').text('支付定金');

        }



        yushouEl.addClass('prebuy-item');

        yushouEl.bind('mouseover',function(){
            $(this).addClass('hover');
        })

        yushouEl.bind('mouseout',function(){
            $(this).removeClass('hover');
        })

    }

}

var imgSize = 'n2';
if ( $('#plist').hasClass('plist-160') ) {
    imgSize = 'n2';
}
if ( $('#plist').hasClass('plist-220') ) {
    if ( $('#plist').hasClass('plist-160') ) {
        imgSize = 'n2';
    } else {
        imgSize = 'n7';
    }
}
if ( $('#plist').hasClass('plist-n7') ) {
    imgSize = 'n7';
}
if ( $('#plist').hasClass('plist-n8') ) {
    imgSize = 'n8';
}
$('.p-scroll').each(function() {
    var scroll = $(this).find('.p-scroll-wrap'),
        btnPrev = $(this).find('.p-scroll-prev'),
        btnNext = $(this).find('.p-scroll-next'),
        len = $(this).find('li').length;
    if ( len > 5 ) {
        btnPrev.css('display', 'inline');
        btnNext.css('display', 'inline');
        scroll.imgScroll({
            visible: 5,
            showControl: false,
            next: btnNext,
            prev: btnPrev
        });
    }
    var colors = scroll.find('img');
    colors.each(function() {
        $(this).mouseover(function() {
            var src = $(this).attr("src"),
                skuid = $(this).attr('data-skuid');
            scroll.find('a').removeClass('curr');
            $(this).parent('a').addClass('curr');
            var targetImg = $(this).parents('li').find('.p-img img').eq(0),
                targetImgLink = $(this).parents('li').find('.p-img a').eq(0),
                targetNameLink = $(this).parents('li').find('.p-name a').eq(0),
                targetFollowLink = $(this).parents('li').find('.product-follow a').eq(0);
            targetImg.attr( 'src', src.replace('\/n5\/', '\/'+imgSize+'\/') );
            targetImgLink.attr( 'href', targetImgLink.attr('href').replace(/\/\d{6,}/, '/'+skuid) );
            targetNameLink.attr( 'href', targetNameLink.attr('href').replace(/\/\d{6,}/, '/'+skuid) );
            targetFollowLink.attr( 'id', targetFollowLink.attr('id').replace(/coll\d{6,}/, 'coll'+skuid) );
        });
    });
});
$('#plist.plist-n7 .list-h>li').hover(function() {
    $(this).addClass('hover').find('.product-follow,.shop-name').show();
    $(this).find('.item-wrap').addClass('item-hover');
}, function() {
    $(this).removeClass('hover').find('.item-wrap').removeClass('item-hover');
    $(this).find('.product-follow,.shop-name').hide();
});

/* 店铺名称 start */
//收集skuId
Array.prototype.unique = function(){
    this.sort();	//先排序
    var res = [this[0]];
    for(var i = 1; i < this.length; i++){
        if(this[i] !== res[res.length - 1]){
            res.push(this[i]);
        }
    }
    return res;
}

var venderIds = [];
$('ul.list-h li[venderId]').each(function(i){
    var venderId = $(this).attr('venderId');
    if(venderId != 0) {
        venderIds.push(venderId);
    }

})

if(venderIds.length > 0) {
    $.ajax({
        url: 'http://d.360buy.com/shop/get?venderids='+venderIds.unique().join(','),
        dataType: 'jsonp',
        success: function(r) {
            if ( !r && !r.length ) { return false; }
            for ( var i = 0; i < r.length; i++ ) {
                var shopInfo =r[i];
                $('ul.list-h li[venderId='+ shopInfo.venderId+']').find('.shop-name').append('<a href="'+ shopInfo.shopUrl+'" target="_blank">'+ shopInfo.shopName+'</a>')
            }
        }
    });
}
